INSTALLING ANSWERPAD:.

- Place the Answerpad folder and it's contents anywhere on my system such as in "My Documents" etc. Answerpad is a simple non-intrusive program that requires no special installation and is easy on my system resources, simply open the folder and click on the exe file to run Answerpad ( file with the book icon ). I can also create a shortcut of the.exe file to my desktop for easier access.

The first time I start Answerpad I will need to make some basic settings either from the "Command" menu or by asking Answerpad to do it for me. Most option settings that I select will remain the default even after exiting for the next time I use Answerpad.

NOTE: 
In order to use MS Agent or DesktopMates characters with Answerpad I must have the required MS Agent components installed on my system. If I have any problems Enabling MSAgent or bringing up the MS Agent character selection window with Answerpad, try installing the required components from here... http://desktopmates.com/agentdownloads.html.

=====================================================================================.

ENABLING MSAGENT:.

- Either choose "Enable Microsoft Agent" from the Command Menu or type "enable agents".

=====================================================================================.

- Either choose "Select Agent Character" from the Command Menu or type "select agent".

=====================================================================================.

CHANGING VOICES:.

=====================================================================================.

ENABLING OPTIONAL SPEECH RECOGNITION:.

- Either choose "Enable speech recognition" from the Command Menu or type "enable speech recognition".

Note: If I want to use speech recognition I will need to install the Microsoft
Speech Recognition Engine which provides speech input capabilities for Microsoft Agent characters which allows I to speak to my character instead of typing. I can download this utility from our MS Agent download page http://desktopmates.com/agentdownloads.html.

Microsoft's speech recognition engine is only available in U.S. English. A certain amount of voice training is required and a decent headset is also highly recommended to filter out background noises. Other third party speech recognition programs may also work but we have not personally tested any others with Answerpad.

SOME IMPORTANT INFO ABOUT USING SPEECH RECOGNITION:.

It's also important to use a decent headset that filters background noises, using a standard mic or poor headsets can cause the program not to be able to understand everything my saying.

For more detailed info about speech recognition refer to this page... http://www.desktopmates.com/speech.html.

=====================================================================================.

SWEAR FILTER:.

Choose "Feel free to swear" from the Command Menu. To stop swearing change back to "Do not swear" from the Command Menu.

=====================================================================================.

OPENING OR STARTING PROGRAMS:.

Answerpad should be able to open most basic programs on my system but there are some programs it may not be able to open, just depends where it's located and on how the program's dll's or registeries are implemented into my system.

Answerpad ca not automatically find or determine where all the programs are located on my system, there are many different types of systems with different directory trees and paths where programs are stored, for example Wordpad is not located in the same directory path on Win98, XP or WindowsMe.

On XP it's usually located here... 
C:\Program Files\Windows NT\Accessories\wordpad.exe.

Do not forget to add the final back slash in front of the file name so it looks like this... C:\Program Files\Invaders\Invaders.exe.

Some programs are more difficult to locate on some systems, if I ca not find the program use my system search and type in something like.... Invaders.* ( the dot after the name with an asterisk will help narrow the search down to only files with that name and that have a file extension such.exe ).

"Run Invaders" will then become the trigger response to open the program. ( quotations are not required when asking to run the program, they are only required when providing the initial statement ).

Test it and once it successfully runs the program be sure to "save memory" before exiting or it will not be stored into Answerpad's database for future reference.

=====================================================================================.

DISPLAYING TEXT OF CONVERSATIONS:.

=====================================================================================.

SAVING my CONVERSATIONS:.

=====================================================================================.

EXITING OPTIONS:.

To exit Answerpad I can use any of the following options.

- Click the "X" like I would to close any window ( be sure to save memory first ).

- Choose "Save memory and exit" from the "File" menu.

- Choose "Exit withot saving memory" from the "File" menu.

- Simply ask by typing or saying "Exit" or "Shutdown" ( be sure to save memory first ).

=====================================================================================.

ADVANCED FEATURE FOR SPECIFYING ANIMATION TRIGGERS:.

The top portion of the txt file lists the character's available animations which are handled internally. The bottom portion allows I to specify up to 100 different words or phrases that will trigger the animation I specify. I will have to play around and experiment with this feature until I get it functioning the way I want.

For reference purposes there's also a list of Rick's available animations provided in the Answerpad directory folder. Animation lists for each DesktopMates character is available on their gallery page on our site which I can view and copy and save into a text file if I wish to have it for reference purposes ( look for the animation list button on the character's gallery page ).

=====================================================================================.

CREATING MULTIPLE BRAIN PERSONALITIES FOR DESKTOPMATES MSAGENT CHARACTERS:.

Answerpad Plus also allows I to create multiple brain personalities. I can have a different brain for each DesktopMates character I have installed.

NOTE: I can edit whatever info I want in the "Memory.Txt", just be sure to leave the top line as is... ** 34563 **. ( this tells Answerpad to reference the character's name ).

To use and switch Characters and brain personalities, go to "MENU" => "FILE" => "CHANGE BOT", a window will appear allowing I to select the character I want which will load the character as well as it's brain.

=====================================================================================.

FINAL NOTES:.

Answerpad Plus has been enhanced by other developers including DesktopMates.com.

Answerpad should be able to open most basic programs on my system but there are some programs it may not be able to open, just depends where it's located and on how the program's dll's or registeries are implemented into my system.

Answerpad ca not automatically find or determine where all the programs are located on my system, there are many different types of systems with different directory trees and paths where programs are stored, for example Wordpad is not located in the same directory path on Win98, XP or WindowsMe.

On XP it's usually located here... 
C:\Program Files\Windows NT\Accessories\wordpad.exe.

Do not forget to add the final back slash in front of the file name so it looks like this... C:\Program Files\Invaders\Invaders.exe.

Some programs are more difficult to locate on some systems, if I ca not find the program use my system search and type in something like.... Invaders.* ( the dot after the name with an asterisk will help narrow the search down to only files with that name and that have a file extension such.exe ).

"Run Invaders" will then become the trigger response to open the program. ( quotations are not required when asking to run the program, they are only required when providing the initial statement ).

Test it and once it successfully runs the program be sure to "save memory" before exiting or it will not be stored into Answerpad's database for future reference.

EXITING OPTIONS:.

To exit Answerpad I can use any of the following options.

- Click the "X" like I would to close any window ( be sure to save memory first ).

- Choose "Save memory and exit" from the "File" menu.

- Choose "Exit withot saving memory" from the "File" menu.

- Simply ask by typing or saying "Exit" or "Shutdown" ( be sure to save memory first ).

=========================
Tips for Using Answerpad
=========================.

INSTALLING ANSWERPAD:.

- Place the Answerpad folder and it's contents anywhere on my system such as in "My Documents" etc. Answerpad is a simple non-intrusive program that requires no special installation and is easy on my system resources, simply open the folder and click on the exe file to run Answerpad ( file with the book icon ). I can also create a shortcut of the.exe file to my desktop for easier access.

The first time I start Answerpad I will need to make some basic settings either from the "Command" menu or by asking Answerpad to do it for me. Most option settings that I select will remain the default even after exiting for the next time I use Answerpad.

NOTE: 
In order to use MS Agent or DesktopMates characters with Answerpad I must have the required MS Agent components installed on my system. If I have any problems Enabling MSAgent or bringing up the MS Agent character selection window with Answerpad, try installing the required components from here... http://desktopmates.com/agentdownloads.html.

=====================================================================================.

ENABLING MSAGENT:.

- Either choose "Enable Microsoft Agent" from the Command Menu or type "enable agents".

=====================================================================================.

- Either choose "Select Agent Character" from the Command Menu or type "select agent".

=====================================================================================.

CHANGING VOICES:.

=====================================================================================.

ENABLING OPTIONAL SPEECH RECOGNITION:.

- Either choose "Enable speech recognition" from the Command Menu or type "enable speech recognition".

Note: If I want to use speech recognition I will need to install the Microsoft
Speech Recognition Engine which provides speech input capabilities for Microsoft Agent characters which allows I to speak to my character instead of typing. I can download this utility from our MS Agent download page http://desktopmates.com/agentdownloads.html.

Microsoft's speech recognition engine is only available in U.S. English. A certain amount of voice training is required and a decent headset is also highly recommended to filter out background noises. Other third party speech recognition programs may also work but we have not personally tested any others with Answerpad.

SOME IMPORTANT INFO ABOUT USING SPEECH RECOGNITION:.

It's also important to use a decent headset that filters background noises, using a standard mic or poor headsets can cause the program not to be able to understand everything my saying.

For more detailed info about speech recognition refer to this page... http://www.desktopmates.com/speech.html.

=====================================================================================.

SWEAR FILTER:.

Choose "Feel free to swear" from the Command Menu. To stop swearing change back to "Do not swear" from the Command Menu.

=====================================================================================.

Most programs like Answerpad work by breaking an user's message down into individual words and then searching through a list of facts for a fact that contains similar words, the fact with the most matching words is used as a response to the user's message. This method is not very good because while it usually replies with a relevant fact, it is not necessarily a fact that answers an users question.

Answerpad works by taking the meaning of words into account, it uses a large table of 'match words' to help it decide which words match or have similar meaning.

Match words Example:
Where=Outside, inside, above, below, near, France, England.
Colour=Red, green, blue, yellow, black.
Thomas=Cat.

Most programs like Answerpad would answer with any fact that contained the word 'cat' because they would simply match the word 'cat' within the question to the word 'cat' within the fact. The words 'Where' and 'Colour' would be totally ignored but these words are crucial to "understanding" the users question.

Below is a list of the main processes names and a brief description of what they do.

BrainCore -
This is the core or root process that uses two timers to call all the other processes.

Speaker -
Text to speech handler, this processes user messages relating to speech and will also speak aloud any of Answerpad's messages.

MSAgent - 
Microsoft's Agent character handler, processes user messages relating to MS Agent and will also speak aloud any of Answerpad's messages. This and the 'text to speech' handler are exclusive of eachother, only one needs to be active.

SpeechRecognizer -
Uses the SAPI speech recognition system to recognize the user's spoken words and handles speech recognition related commands.

EasyInput -
The window for letting kids select words with a mouse.

MemoryForm -
The window that displays the contents of Answerpad's memory. This feature is hidden from the user, but 'sm666' is the command to display it.

HistoryForm -
A window for showing the most recent messages.

Help1 -
Shows the readme.txt file that is stored within Answerpad's folder.

Other processes:.

Interface -
This is the main interface window and contains the code for handling things like the fading text messages and menus.

About1 -
The about window.

ListForm - 		
This is used for displaying lists of options, for example the text to speech handler will use this form to display available speech engines.

Progress - 
Progress bar, used when loading fact files.

Splash -
Displays the Answerpad startup screen when loading.

The code is not heavily commented because you have always relied on large labels to help describe a function. Most functions will have a comment at the start that explains what the function does.

Editing Answerpad's Memory File.

When I open Answerpad's memory file in a text editor I will notice at that at the end there is a huge list of words, these are known as match words. when Answerpad searches it is memory for a relevant response it does not just compare words within the user's question to words stored in a fact, it will take into account synonyms or 'match words' and will also compare these words.

Application software is contrasted with system software and middleware, which manage and integrate a computer's capabilities, but typically do not directly apply in the performance of tasks that benefit the user. The system software serves the application, which in turn serves the user.

Similar relationships apply in other fields. For example, a shopping mall does not provide the merchandise a shopper is seeking, but provides space and services for retailers that serve the shopper. A bridge may similarly support rail tracks which support trains, allowing the trains to transport passengers.

With the spread of smartphones and tablet computers around 2010, the short form app was in some popular news accounts restricted to mobile apps.

Application software falls into two general categories; horizontal applications and vertical applications. Horizontal applications are the most popular and widespread in departments or companies. Vertical applications are niche products, designed for a particular type of business or division in a company.

There are many types of application software:.

Applications can also be classified by computing platform such as a particular operating system, delivery network such as in cloud computing and Web 2.0 applications, or delivery devices such as mobile apps for mobile devices.

The operating system itself can be considered application software when performing simple calculating, measuring, rendering, and word processing tasks not used to control hardware via command-line interface or graphical user interface. This does not include application software bundled within operating systems such as a software calculator or text editor.

Takeaway: European research lab Cern today announced a landmark discovery for physics. TechRepublic explores the technology used in the hunt for the Higgs Boson particle.

The centuries old question of why the universe has mass may be one step closer to being answered.

Today the European nuclear physics lab Cern announced it has discovered a particle that fits the bill for the elusive Higgs Boson - the theoretical particle thought to be responsible for generating mass.

If it is the Higgs it will be the final missing ingredient in the Standard Model of particle physics, the theory which explains all known particles and the forces that act upon them.

The candidate particle was identified by experiments inside the labï¿½s Large Hadron Collider ( LHC ) particle accelerator - which bangs together sub-atomic particles at close to the speed of light and then analyses the resulting debris. The energy of these collisions is equivalent to that billionths of a second after the Big Bang.

The ATLAS and CMS detectors inside the LHC have observed the new particle at mass ranges of 125 - 126 gigaelectronvolts ( GeV ) - many times heavier than than the neutron inside the atom and within the mass range predicted for the Higgs Boson.

The lab is cross-checking the results of the experiment before publishing, although apparently the chance of the result being a fluke is no more than one in two million.

4.3.1 The Root Element
Contained By:	As the root element of a document.
Wherever a subdocument fragment is allowed in a compound document.
Content Model:	A head element followed by a body element.
Attributes
Global attributes
manifest	DOM Interface
Uses HTMLElement.

Not today, today you had I read about html.

Different also can mean not the same topic.

That did not work.

The html element is the root element of a document. Every document must begin with this element, and it must contain both the head and body elements.

It is considered good practice to specify the primary language of the document on this element using the lang attribute.

HTML Example:
<DOCTYPE html>
<html lang= "en" >
 <head>
...
 </head>
 <body>
...
 </body>
</html>.

In the HTML syntax only, both the start and end tags are optional, and so for convenience either may be omitted, unless I wish to specify attributes on this element, in which case, at least the start tag needs to be included.

In the XHTML syntax, the xmlns attribute needs to be specified on this element to declare that it is in the HTML namespace. I may use either the lang or xml:lang attribute to specify the langauge.

XHTML Example:
<html xmlns= "http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml" xml:lang= "en" >
 <head>
...
 </head>
 <body>
...
 </body>
</html>
manifest
The manifest attribute gives the address of the documentï¿½s application cache manifest, if there is one. If the attribute is present, the attributeï¿½s value must be a valid URL.

4.3.2 Document Metadata
4.3.2.1 The head element.

The head element collects the documentï¿½s metadata.
Start tag: optional End tag: optional Categories:	None.
Contained By:	As the first element in an html element.
Content Model:	One or more elements of metadata content, of which exactly one is a title element.
Attributes
Global attributes	DOM Interface
Uses HTMLElement.

The head element is the container for the documentï¿½s metadata. Metadata is information about the document itself, such as it's title, author. Scripts and stylesheets may also be included within the head element. Every document must have a head element.

The following examples illustrate the typical usage of the head element in HTML and XHTML.

HTML Example
<DOCTYPE html>
<html>
<head>
 <title>Example</title>
</head>
<body>
 <h1>Document</h1>
</body>
</html>.

XHTML Example
<html xmlns= "http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml" >
<head>
 <title>Example</title>
</head>
<body>
 <h1>Document</h1>
</body>
</html>.

4.3.2.2 The title element.

The title element represents the documentï¿½s title or name, and should be meaningful even when read out of context.
Start tag: required End tag: required Categories:	Metadata content.
Contained By:	In a head element containing no other title elements.
Content Model:	Text.

He ordered cognac and croissants
He made a mental list
Of things he owned but did not want
All the buildings, all the real estate
The antique glass and stone
He would trade a vow of poverty
To see the angel of Lyon.

Or at least the parts he knew
And watched the shadow of the train
On the towns that they rolled through
And he closed his eyes and he saw two rivers
The Rhone and the saone
The male and female spirit of
The city of Lyon.

Then he waited on the bridge
Where they met the year before
But the days turned into weeks
And then the seasons numbered four
And his clothes grew worn and ragged
As through that town he roamed
Searching every open window
For the angel of Lyon.

The Rhone and the saone
They would not give up the secret of
The angel of Lyon.

In the basilica tonight
Where sister eve maria
Is the keeper of the light

Walks a saint of rag and bone
The madman torn asunder
By the angel of lyon.

The role of Artificial Intelligence has increased over the past few years with it is application cutting across different sectors from finance to retail and health industries.

Over the last few years, the terms Machine Learning and Deep Learning have gained popularity where artificial intelligence is discussed. These phrases are sometimes used interchangeably however, they have different meanings.

Artificial intelligence is a subsection of computer science. This term was created by John McCarthy in 1956. He defined it as the science and engineering of making intelligent machines.

AI is any intelligence, characteristically human, demonstrated by a machine or computer in solving a problem it is given.

MACHINE LEARNING. This involves training a machine using a large amount of data and algorithms that enable it to make a forecast about something. Without machine learning, AI can still function but it would require inputting many lines of code with particular instructions to carry out a task and this process can be complex and cumbersome. With machine learning, information is fed, the machine learns the patterns and trends, it adjusts and improves.

A system with this capability gets increasingly better at performing a certain function.

DEEP LEARNING is a subset of Machine Learning. It works using the Artificial Neural Network ( ANN ). ANN is a system based on how neurons in the brains connect and function. The network is designed to continuously analyze data and learn a structure similar to how humans reason and draw conclusions. The neural network has discrete layers and connections to each other; each layer is designed to learn a particular task.

This layering is where the name deep learning is derived. An example of this is a self-driving car. Each layer of this model would learn a certain task such as recognizing a pedestrian or identifying street signs. A combination of these different tasks will enable it to navigate the streets.

Artificial Intelligence is a generic term for intelligence displayed by machines. Machine Learning ( ML ) is one way to attain AI and deep learning is an advancement of machine learning. ML and DL require a large volume of data to work with. This data can be used from the Internet of Things ( IoT ) which is the growing network of physical devices e.g. smartphones, appliances, vehicles, machines that are accessible via the internet.

The relationship between Artificial Intelligence and the Internet of Things is complimentary. AI uses the information from IoT as it needs data to work and AI becomes reliable due to information from IoT. With both advancing rapidly, the possibilities are endless.

The following steps determine if the AI chatbot that learns is intelligent:.

Firstly, the AI chatbot has to identify the goal for a specific situation.

Then it has to process the available information to see if the goal can be realized, if not, it has to request for more information this involves sensing the environment where it resides in order to perform a set of given tasks.

Based on this information, it has to go on recursive mode to see if the goal can be realized or not. This involves thinking or making decisions based on the environment.

Usually, the requests or responses from users are converted into a machine-understandable form and stored in the form of parameter values in the information base from which it is retrieved from time to time.

A system of continuous knowledge-building is followed by the interactive system which influences it is learning capacity. This knowledge base helps the chatbot learn faster, identify relevant information for faster response time, and provide the most convincing response based on it is decision-making caliber built over time.

The AI chatbot then acts by carrying out it is decisions
A certain level of predictive analysis is built over time with the increasing number of human interactions and queries stored in the information repository which helps the AI chatbot that learns to plan ahead about the queries that would come from the userâs end.
